<script>
// Task 39: Noindex search result pages
(function() {
  var params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
  if (params.has('q') || params.has('search') || params.has('page')) {
    var metaRobots = document.querySelector('meta[name="robots"]');
    if (metaRobots) {
      metaRobots.content = 'noindex, follow';
    } else {
      var meta = document.createElement('meta');
      meta.name = 'robots';
      meta.content = 'noindex, follow';
      document.head.appendChild(meta);
    }
  }
})();
</script>

function toggleMobileNav(){
  const nav=document.getElementById('mobileNav');
  const btn=document.getElementById('hamburger');
  nav.classList.toggle('open');
  btn.classList.toggle('open');
  document.body.style.overflow=nav.classList.contains('open')?'hidden':'';
}

let lang=(()=>{
  try{const s=localStorage.getItem('swiftswap_lang');if(s&&['en','tr','es','de','fr','ru','zh','ja','ko','pt','ar','it'].includes(s))return s;}catch(e){}
  return 'en';
})();
function t(k){return (S[lang]||S.en)[k]||S.en[k]||k;}
function applyLang(){
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-i18n]').forEach(el=>{
    const v=t(el.getAttribute('data-i18n'));
    if(typeof v==='string'&&v.includes('<em>')){el.innerHTML=v;}
    else if(el.tagName==='BUTTON'||el.tagName==='A'){el.textContent=v;}
    else{el.innerHTML=v;}
  });
  // sync lang button label/flag with current lang (was only set inside setLang())
  const _curL=LANGS.find(x=>x.code===lang);
  if(_curL){
    const _cf=document.getElementById('curFlag');if(_cf)_cf.textContent=_curL.flag;
    const _cn=document.getElementById('curLangName');if(_cn)_cn.textContent=_curL.name;
  }
  document.documentElement.lang=lang;
  document.body && (document.body.style.direction=lang==='ar'?'rtl':'ltr');
  const _addr=document.getElementById('addrLbl');if(_addr)_addr.textContent=t('addr_lbl');
  const _cb=document.getElementById('cookie-text');if(_cb)_cb.innerHTML='🍪 '+t('cookie_text')+' <a href="/privacy.html">'+t('cookie_link')+'</a>';
  const _ca=document.getElementById('cookie-accept');if(_ca)_ca.textContent=t('cookie_accept');
  document.querySelectorAll('.feat-ttl')[0] && (() => {
    const ftts=document.querySelectorAll('.feat-ttl');
    const fds=document.querySelectorAll('.feat-desc');
    if(ftts[0]){ftts[0].textContent=t('feat1_title');fds[0].textContent=t('feat1_desc');}
    if(ftts[1]){ftts[1].textContent=t('feat2_title');fds[1].textContent=t('feat2_desc');}
    if(ftts[2]){ftts[2].textContent=t('feat3_title');fds[2].textContent=t('feat3_desc');}
  })();
  renderFAQ();
}
function setLang(code){
  lang=code;
  const l=LANGS.find(x=>x.code===code);
  if(!l) return;
  document.getElementById('curFlag').textContent=l.flag;
  document.getElementById('curLangName').textContent=l.name;
  document.querySelectorAll('.lang-opt').forEach(el=>el.classList.toggle('active',el.dataset.code===code));
  document.getElementById('langSel').classList.remove('open');
  document.documentElement.lang=code;
  const localeMap={en:'en_US',tr:'tr_TR',es:'es_ES',de:'de_DE',fr:'fr_FR',ru:'ru_RU',zh:'zh_CN',ja:'ja_JP',ko:'ko_KR',pt:'pt_BR',ar:'ar_SA',it:'it_IT'};
  const ogL=document.getElementById('ogLocale');if(ogL)ogL.setAttribute('content',localeMap[code]||'en_US');
  document.body.style.direction=code==='ar'?'rtl':'ltr';
  try{localStorage.setItem('swiftswap_lang',code);}catch(e){}
  applyLang();
}
function toggleLang(e){e.stopPropagation();document.getElementById('langSel').classList.toggle('open');}
function buildLangDd(){
  document.getElementById('langDd').innerHTML=LANGS.map(l=>`<div class="lang-opt ${l.code===lang?'active':''}" data-code="${l.code}" onclick="setLang('${l.code}')"><span style="font-size:18px;">${l.flag}</span><div><div class="lang-nm">${l.name}</div><div class="lang-nat">${l.native}</div></div></div>`).join('');
}
document.addEventListener('click',e=>{
  if(!e.target.closest('.lang-sel'))document.getElementById('langSel').classList.remove('open');
  if(!e.target.closest('.swap-box'))document.querySelectorAll('.c-dd').forEach(d=>d.classList.remove('open'));
});

/* ─── BACKEND CONFIG ─── */
const BACKEND_URL = ''; // Same-domain proxy via nginx
let csrfToken = null;
async function fetchCsrfToken() {
  try {
    const r = await fetch('/api/csrf-token');
    const d = await r.json();
    if (d.success) csrfToken = d.token;
  } catch(e) { console.warn('CSRF fetch failed:', e); }
}
fetchCsrfToken();
function csrfHeaders() {
  const h = {'Content-Type': 'application/json'};
  if (csrfToken) h['x-csrf-token'] = csrfToken;
  return h;
}

let prices=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(FALLBACK));
let sendC=COINS[0], recvC=COINS[1], rateType='fixed';

function fmt(n){if(!n||isNaN(n))return'0';if(n>=1e9)return(n/1e9).toFixed(2)+'B';if(n>=1e6)return(n/1e6).toFixed(2)+'M';if(n>=1000)return n.toLocaleString('en-US',{maximumFractionDigits:2});if(n>=1)return n.toFixed(2);if(n>=0.01)return n.toFixed(4);return n.toFixed(8);}
function gp(c){return prices[c.id]?.usd||0;}

async function loadRates(spin=false){
  if(spin){const b=document.getElementById('refBtn');b.classList.add('spinning');setTimeout(()=>b.classList.remove('spinning'),800);}
  try{
    const ids=COINS.slice(0,20).map(c=>c.id).join(','); // SwiftSwap Data free tier: max 20
    const r=await fetch(`/api/prices?ids=${ids}&vs=usd&include_market_cap=true&include_24hr_vol=true`);
    if(!r.ok)throw new Error();
    prices=await r.json();
    document.getElementById('apiSt').textContent='Live Rates';
    document.getElementById('lastUpd').textContent='Updated '+new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
  }catch{
    document.getElementById('apiSt').textContent='Cached';
    document.getElementById('lastUpd').textContent='Using cached data';
  }
  renderMarket();renderTicker();recalc();
  return true;
}

let recalcTimer=null;
let lastRate=null;

function recalc(){
  // Anlık USD gösterimi (SwiftSwap Data'dan)
  const sp=gp(sendC),rp=gp(recvC);
  const a=parseFloat(document.getElementById('sendAmt').value)||0;
  if(a>0&&sp) document.getElementById('sendUsd').textContent=`≈ $${fmt(a*sp)} USD`;
  else document.getElementById('sendUsd').textContent='';

  // Backend rate debounce (500ms bekle, sonra çek)
  clearTimeout(recalcTimer);
  if(!a||a<=0){ 
    document.getElementById('recvAmt').value='';
    document.getElementById('recvUsd').textContent='';
    document.getElementById('rateV').textContent='—';
    return;
  }
  document.getElementById('recvAmt').value='...';
  document.getElementById('rateV').textContent='Fetching rate...';
  recalcTimer=setTimeout(()=>fetchBackendRate(a),500);
}

async function fetchBackendRate(amount){
  try{
    const r=await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/rate`,{
      method:'POST',
      headers:csrfHeaders(),
      body:JSON.stringify({
        fromCurrency:sendC.sym.toLowerCase(),
        toCurrency:recvC.sym.toLowerCase(),
        fromAmount:amount,
        fromNetwork:sendC.cnNetwork||undefined,
        toNetwork:recvC.cnNetwork||undefined,
        rateType:rateType
      })
    });
    const data=await r.json();
    if(!data.success){
      if(data.error&&(data.error.includes('min')||data.error.includes('low'))){
        document.getElementById('recvAmt').value='';
        document.getElementById('rateV').textContent='Below minimum amount';
        return;
      }
      throw new Error(data.error||'Rate error');
    }
    lastRate=data;
    const netAmt=parseFloat(data.toAmount);
    document.getElementById('recvAmt').value=netAmt.toFixed(8);
    const commPct=rateType==='float'?'1%':'1.5%';
    document.getElementById('rateV').textContent=`1 ${sendC.sym} = ${(netAmt/amount).toFixed(4)} ${recvC.sym}`;
    const rp=gp(recvC);
    if(rp&&netAmt) document.getElementById('recvUsd').innerHTML=`<span style="color:var(--accent);">≈ $${fmt(netAmt*rp)} USD</span>`;
    document.getElementById('apiSt').textContent='Live Rates';
    document.getElementById('rateU').textContent=`${commPct} fee`;
    // Fee breakdown kartı
    const raw=parseFloat(data.rawToAmount)||netAmt;
    const wFee=parseFloat(data.withdrawalFee)||0;
    const ourFee=parseFloat(data.commissionAmount)||0;
    const sp=gp(sendC)||0;
    const bd=document.getElementById('feeBreakdown');
    if(raw&&(wFee||ourFee)){
      bd.style.display='block';
      document.getElementById('fbMarket').textContent=sp?`${(amount*sp).toFixed(2)} ${recvC.sym}≈`:`${raw.toFixed(4)} ${recvC.sym}`;
      const fbNetRow=document.getElementById('fbNetRow');
      if(wFee>0){
        fbNetRow.style.display='flex';
        document.getElementById('fbNet').textContent=`-${wFee.toFixed(4)} ${recvC.sym}`;
      } else {
        fbNetRow.style.display='none';
      }
      document.getElementById('fbPct').textContent=commPct;
      document.getElementById('fbOurs').textContent=`-${ourFee.toFixed(4)} ${recvC.sym}`;
      document.getElementById('fbFinal').textContent=`${netAmt.toFixed(4)} ${recvC.sym}`;
    } else {
      bd.style.display='none';
    }
  }catch(e){
    // Backend kapalıysa SwiftSwap Data ile fallback
    const sp=gp(sendC),rp=gp(recvC);
    if(sp&&rp){
      const fee=rateType==='fixed'?0.01:0.005;
      const res=amount*(sp/rp)*(1-fee);
      document.getElementById('recvAmt').value=res>0?res.toFixed(8):'';
      document.getElementById('rateV').textContent=`1 ${sendC.sym} ≈ ${(sp/rp).toFixed(6)} ${recvC.sym}`;
      document.getElementById('apiSt').textContent='Est. Rate';
    }
    console.warn('Backend rate fetch failed, using fallback:', e.message);
  }
}
function setType(tp){rateType=tp;document.getElementById('fixedBtn').classList.toggle('active',tp==='fixed');document.getElementById('floatBtn').classList.toggle('active',tp==='float');recalc();}
function swapCoins(){[sendC,recvC]=[recvC,sendC];setCoinUI('send',sendC);setCoinUI('recv',recvC);updatePh();recalc();}
function setCoinUI(side,c){
  document.getElementById(side+'Ico').style.background=c.color;
  document.getElementById(side+'Ico').textContent=c.sym[0];
  document.getElementById(side+'Sym').textContent=c.sym;
  document.getElementById(side+'Nm').textContent=c.network||c.name;
}
function updatePh(){
  document.getElementById('addrInp').placeholder=recvC.ph||'Enter address...';
  document.getElementById('addrLbl').textContent=`${recvC.sym} Recipient Address (${recvC.network})`;
}
function openDrop(id){document.querySelectorAll('.c-dd').forEach(d=>{if(d.id!==id)d.classList.remove('open');});document.getElementById(id).classList.toggle('open');}
function buildList(listId,ddId){
  const isSend=ddId==='sendDd';
  document.getElementById(listId).innerHTML=COINS.map(c=>{
    const p=gp(c);
    return `<div class="c-opt" onclick="selCoin('${c.sym}','${ddId}')">
      <div class="c-ico" style="background:${c.color};width:30px;height:30px;">${c.sym[0]}</div>
      <div><div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700;">${c.sym}</div><div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);">${c.name}</div></div>
      <div class="c-opt-p">${p?'$'+fmt(p):''}</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}
function filterList(inp,listId){const q=inp.value.toLowerCase();document.getElementById(listId).querySelectorAll('.c-opt').forEach(el=>{el.style.display=el.textContent.toLowerCase().includes(q)?'':'none';});}
function selCoin(sym,ddId){
  const c=COINS.find(x=>x.sym===sym);if(!c)return;
  if(ddId==='sendDd'){if(c.sym===recvC.sym)recvC=sendC;sendC=c;setCoinUI('send',sendC);setCoinUI('recv',recvC);}
  else{if(c.sym===sendC.sym)sendC=recvC;recvC=c;setCoinUI('recv',recvC);setCoinUI('send',sendC);}
  document.getElementById(ddId).classList.remove('open');
  updatePh();recalc();
}
// Normalize address: EVM addresses to lowercase (fixes EIP-55 checksum issues with ChangeNOW)
function normalizeAddr(addr, coin){
  if(!addr) return addr;
  // EVM chains: ETH, BNB, MATIC, USDC(ERC20), etc — starts with 0x
  if(addr.startsWith('0x') || addr.startsWith('0X')) return addr.toLowerCase();
  return addr.trim();
}

async function doExchange(){
  const rawAddr=document.getElementById('addrInp').value.trim();
  const addr=normalizeAddr(rawAddr, recvC.sym);
  const amt=parseFloat(document.getElementById('sendAmt').value);
  const out=document.getElementById('recvAmt').value;

  // Validation
  if(!addr){
    document.getElementById('addrInp').style.borderColor='var(--red)';
    setTimeout(()=>document.getElementById('addrInp').style.borderColor='',2000);
    showToast('⚠️ Please enter a recipient wallet address.');return;
  }
  if(!amt||amt<=0){showToast('⚠️ Please enter an amount.');return;}
  if(out==='...'||!out){showToast('⚠️ Please wait for rate to load.');return;}

  // Button loading state
  const btn=document.querySelector('.ex-btn');
  btn.disabled=true;
  btn.innerHTML='<span>Processing... ⏳</span>';

  try{
    const r=await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/create`,{
      method:'POST',
      headers:csrfHeaders(),
      body:JSON.stringify({
        fromCurrency:sendC.sym.toLowerCase(),
        toCurrency:recvC.sym.toLowerCase(),
        fromAmount:amt,
        toAddress:addr,
        fromNetwork:sendC.cnNetwork||undefined,
        toNetwork:recvC.cnNetwork||undefined,
        rateType:rateType
      })
    });
    const data=await r.json();
    if(!data.success) throw new Error(data.error||'Exchange failed');

    // Show payment modal
    showPaymentScreen(data, amt, out, addr);

  }catch(e){
    const msg=e.message||'';
    if(msg.includes('too low')||msg.includes('min amount')){
      showToast('⚠️ Amount is below minimum. Please enter a higher amount.');
    } else if(msg.includes('address')||msg.includes('checksum')){
      showToast('⚠️ Invalid wallet address. Please check and try again.');
    } else if(msg.includes('restricted')||msg.includes('sanctioned')){
      showToast('❌ This address is restricted and cannot be used.');
    } else {
      showToast('❌ '+(msg||'Could not create exchange. Check your connection.'));
    }
    console.error('Exchange error:',e);
  }finally{
    btn.disabled=false;
    btn.innerHTML='<span data-i18n="btn_exchange">Exchange Now ⚡</span>';
  }
}

function showPaymentScreen(order, sendAmt, recvAmt, toAddr){
  const modal=document.getElementById('paymentModal');
  document.getElementById('pm-orderId').textContent=order.orderId||order.id||'—';
  document.getElementById('pm-sendAmt').textContent=`${sendAmt} ${sendC.sym}`;
  document.getElementById('pm-recvAmt').textContent=`${parseFloat(recvAmt).toFixed(6)} ${recvC.sym}`;
  document.getElementById('pm-toAddr').textContent=toAddr.slice(0,12)+'...'+toAddr.slice(-8);
  const pAddr=order.payinAddress||'';
  document.getElementById('pm-payinAddr').textContent=pAddr||'—';
  document.getElementById('pm-payinAddrFull').value=pAddr;
  document.getElementById('pm-network').textContent=sendC.sym+' ('+sendC.network+') Network';
  document.getElementById('pm-exactAmt').textContent=`${order.payinAmount||sendAmt} ${sendC.sym}`;
  // QR code via api.qrserver.com
  if(pAddr){
    const qrImg=document.getElementById('pm-qr');
    if(qrImg) qrImg.src=`https://api.qrserver.com/v1/create-qr-code/?size=200x200&margin=0&color=000000&bgcolor=ffffff&data=${encodeURIComponent(pAddr)}`;
  }
  // Reset status + steps
  const statusEl=document.getElementById('pm-status');
  if(statusEl){statusEl.textContent='⏳ Waiting for deposit';statusEl.style.color='#f59e0b';}
  document.querySelectorAll('.pm-step').forEach((el,i)=>{
    el.classList.remove('pm-step-done','pm-step-active','pm-step-pending');
    el.classList.add(i===0?'pm-step-active':'pm-step-pending');
  });
  const depBox=document.getElementById('pm-depositBox');
  if(depBox) depBox.style.display='';
  const txRow=document.getElementById('pm-txHashRow');
  if(txRow) txRow.style.display='none';
  modal.style.display='flex';
  startPmTimer();
  if(order.orderId) startOrderPolling(order.orderId);
}

let pollingInterval=null;
let currentOrderData=null;

function startOrderPolling(orderId){
  clearInterval(pollingInterval);
  let checks=0;
  pollingInterval=setInterval(async()=>{
    checks++;
    if(checks>120){clearInterval(pollingInterval);return;} // 30 dk sonra dur (120 * 15s)
    try{
      const r=await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/status/${orderId}`);
      const data=await r.json();
      if(!data.success) return;
      updateOrderStatus(data.status, data);
      if(['finished','failed','refunded'].includes(data.status)){
        clearInterval(pollingInterval);
      }
    }catch(e){console.warn('Status poll failed:',e);}
  },15000); // 15 saniyede bir kontrol
}

const STATUS_STEPS=['waiting','confirming','exchanging','sending','finished'];
function updateOrderStatus(status, data){
  const statusMap={
    waiting:    {label:'Waiting for deposit',    color:'#f59e0b', icon:'⏳', step:0},
    confirming: {label:'Confirming transaction', color:'#3b82f6', icon:'🔍', step:1},
    exchanging: {label:'Exchanging',             color:'#a855f7', icon:'⚡', step:2},
    sending:    {label:'Sending to you',         color:'#22c55e', icon:'🚀', step:3},
    finished:   {label:'Completed!',             color:'#22c55e', icon:'✅', step:4},
    failed:     {label:'Failed',                 color:'#ef4444', icon:'❌', step:-1},
    refunded:   {label:'Refunded',               color:'#f59e0b', icon:'↩️', step:-1},
  };
  const s=statusMap[status]||{label:status,color:'var(--text2)',icon:'•',step:0};

  // Update status text
  const el=document.getElementById('pm-status');
  if(el){ el.textContent=s.icon+' '+s.label; el.style.color=s.color; }

  // Update progress steps
  const stepEls=document.querySelectorAll('.pm-step');
  stepEls.forEach((el,i)=>{
    el.classList.remove('pm-step-done','pm-step-active','pm-step-pending');
    if(s.step>i) el.classList.add('pm-step-done');
    else if(s.step===i) el.classList.add('pm-step-active');
    else el.classList.add('pm-step-pending');
  });

  if(status==='finished'){
    showFinishedScreen(data);
  }
  if(status==='failed'||status==='refunded'){
    const depBox=document.getElementById('pm-depositBox');
    if(depBox) depBox.style.display='none';
  }
  if(data?.payoutHash){
    const txEl=document.getElementById('pm-txHash');
    const txRow=document.getElementById('pm-txHashRow');
    if(txEl){ txEl.textContent=data.payoutHash.slice(0,20)+'...'; }
    if(txRow){ txRow.style.display='flex'; }
  }
}

function showFinishedScreen(data){
  const modal=document.getElementById('paymentModal');
  const inner=document.getElementById('pm-inner');
  if(!inner) return;
  const sendAmt=document.getElementById('pm-sendAmt').textContent;
  const recvAmt=document.getElementById('pm-recvAmt').textContent;
  inner.innerHTML=`
    <div style="text-align:center;padding:24px 0;">
      <div style="font-size:72px;margin-bottom:8px;animation:popIn .5s cubic-bezier(.34,1.56,.64,1);">🎉</div>
      <div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:800;color:#22c55e;margin-bottom:6px;">Exchange Complete!</div>
      <div style="font-size:14px;color:var(--text2);margin-bottom:24px;">Your funds are on the way</div>
      <div style="background:rgba(34,197,94,.08);border:1px solid rgba(34,197,94,.2);border-radius:14px;padding:20px;margin-bottom:20px;text-align:left;">
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:10px;">
          <span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text3);">Sent</span>
          <span style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:13px;font-weight:700;">${sendAmt}</span>
        </div>
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;">
          <span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text3);">Received</span>
          <span style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#22c55e;">${recvAmt}</span>
        </div>
        ${data?.payoutHash?`<div style="margin-top:10px;padding-top:10px;border-top:1px solid var(--border);">
          <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);margin-bottom:4px;">TX Hash</div>
          <div style="font-family:var(--mono);font-size:11px;color:#22c55e;word-break:break-all;">${data.payoutHash}</div>
        </div>`:''}
      </div>
      <button onclick="closePaymentModal()" style="width:100%;padding:14px;background:#22c55e;border:none;border-radius:12px;color:#000;font-weight:700;font-size:15px;cursor:pointer;font-family:'DM Sans',sans-serif;box-shadow:0 4px 24px rgba(34,197,94,.3);">
        Done ✓
      </button>
      <div style="margin-top:12px;font-size:13px;color:var(--text3);">Thank you for using SwiftSwap!</div>
    </div>
  `;
}
function showToast(msg){const t=document.getElementById('toast');document.getElementById('toastMsg').textContent=msg;t.classList.add('show');setTimeout(()=>t.classList.remove('show'),4500);}

/* MARKET */
function renderMarket(){
  document.getElementById('mktBody').innerHTML=COINS.slice(0,12).map((c,i)=>{
    const d=prices[c.id]||{};const ch=d.usd_24h_change||0;
    return `<div class="mkt-row" style="animation-delay:${i*0.04}s;">
      <div class="mkt-rank">${i+1}</div>
      <div class="mkt-coin"><div style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:50%;background:${c.color};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:white;">${c.sym[0]}</div><div><div class="mkt-sym">${c.sym}</div><div class="mkt-fn">${c.name}</div></div></div>
      <div class="mkt-price">$${fmt(d.usd||0)}</div>
      <div class="mkt-chg ${ch>=0?'up':'dn'}">${ch>=0?'+':''}${ch.toFixed(2)}%</div>
      <div class="mkt-cap">$${fmt(d.usd_market_cap||0)}</div>
      <div class="mkt-vol">$${fmt(d.usd_24h_vol||0)}</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}



/* TICKER */
function renderTicker(){
  const TICKER_ICONS = {BTC:'₿',ETH:'Ξ',SOL:'◎',BNB:'⬡',USDT:'₮',USDC:'$',XRP:'✕',ADA:'₳',DOGE:'Ð',DOT:'●',AVAX:'▲',MATIC:'⬡',LINK:'⬡',UNI:'🦄',LTC:'Ł',BCH:'₿'};
  const items=COINS.filter(c=>prices[c.id]).slice(0,14).map(c=>{
    const d=prices[c.id];const ch=d.usd_24h_change||0;
    const ico=TICKER_ICONS[c.sym]||'•';
    return `<div class="ticker-item"><span class="ticker-sym">${ico} ${c.sym}</span><span class="ticker-price">$${fmt(d.usd)}</span><span class="${ch>=0?'t-up':'t-dn'}">${ch>=0?'▲':'▼'}${Math.abs(ch).toFixed(2)}%</span></div>`;
  }).join('');
  const tr=document.getElementById('tickerTrack');tr.innerHTML=items+items;
}

/* TX */
function timeAgo(iso){
  const diff=Math.floor((Date.now()-new Date(iso).getTime())/1000);
  if(diff<60)return diff+'s ago';
  if(diff<3600)return Math.floor(diff/60)+'m ago';
  if(diff<86400)return Math.floor(diff/3600)+'h ago';
  return Math.floor(diff/86400)+'d ago';
}
function renderTXData(txs){
  const el=document.getElementById('txBody');
  if(!el)return;
  el.innerHTML=txs.map((tx,i)=>{
    const f=tx.fromCurrency||tx.f,to=tx.toCurrency||tx.t;
    const fc=COINS.find(c=>c.sym===f)||{color:'#555'};
    const tc=COINS.find(c=>c.sym===to)||{color:'#555'};
    const amt=tx.payinAmount?tx.payinAmount+' '+f:(tx.a||'');
    const tm=tx.createdAt?timeAgo(tx.createdAt):(tx.tm||'');
    const st=tx.status||'waiting';
    const ok=st==='finished'||st==='sending'||st==='done'||st===true;
    const wait=st==='waiting'||st==='confirming'||st===false;
    return `<div class="tx-row" style="animation-delay:${i*0.05}s;"><div class="tx-pr"><div style="width:22px;height:22px;border-radius:50%;background:${fc.color};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:9px;font-weight:700;color:white;">${f[0]}</div><span class="tx-ar">→</span><div style="width:22px;height:22px;border-radius:50%;background:${tc.color};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:9px;font-weight:700;color:white;">${to[0]}</div><span>${f}→${to}</span></div><div class="tx-amt">${amt}</div><div class="tx-tm">${tm}</div><div><span class="badge ${ok?'b-ok':'b-wait'}">${ok?'✓ Done':'⏳ Wait'}</span></div></div>`;
  }).join('');
}
async function renderTX(){
  try{
    const r=await fetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/recent-transactions`);
    if(r.ok){
      const d=await r.json();
      if(d.transactions&&d.transactions.length>0){renderTXData(d.transactions);return;}
    }
  }catch(e){}
  // fallback static data
  renderTXData([{f:'BTC',t:'ETH',a:'0.12 BTC',tm:'2m ago',ok:true},{f:'USDT',t:'SOL',a:'500 USDT',tm:'5m ago',ok:true},{f:'ETH',t:'BNB',a:'2.5 ETH',tm:'8m ago',ok:true},{f:'LTC',t:'USDT',a:'1 LTC',tm:'12m ago',ok:false},{f:'BNB',t:'USDT',a:'3 BNB',tm:'18m ago',ok:true}]);
}

/* FAQ */
function renderFAQ(){
  document.getElementById('faqList').innerHTML=[['faq1_q','faq1_a'],['faq2_q','faq2_a'],['faq3_q','faq3_a'],['faq4_q','faq4_a'],['faq5_q','faq5_a'],['faq6_q','faq6_a'],['faq7_q','faq7_a'],['faq8_q','faq8_a'],['faq9_q','faq9_a'],['faq10_q','faq10_a']].map(([q,a])=>`<div class="faq-item"><div class="faq-q" onclick="this.parentElement.classList.toggle('open')"><span>${t(q)}</span><span class="faq-ico">▼</span></div><div class="faq-a">${t(a)}</div></div>`).join('');
}

/* CARD LIVE BALANCE */
function updateCardBalance(){
  const btc=prices['bitcoin']?.usd||67200;
  const fakeBtc=0.1482;
  const usdVal=(fakeBtc*btc).toLocaleString('en-US',{maximumFractionDigits:2});
  const el=document.getElementById('cardBtcBal');
  if(el) el.textContent=fakeBtc+' BTC ≈ $'+usdVal;
}

      <input type="email" id="notifyEmail" placeholder="your@email.com" style="flex:1;padding:11px 14px;background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;color:var(--text);font-size:14px;outline:none;font-family:'DM Sans',sans-serif;" onfocus="this.style.borderColor='rgba(34,197,94,.5)'" onblur="this.style.borderColor='var(--border)'">
      <button onclick="submitNotify()" style="padding:11px 18px;background:var(--accent);border:none;border-radius:10px;color:#000;font-weight:700;font-size:14px;cursor:pointer;font-family:'DM Sans',sans-serif;white-space:nowrap;">Notify Me</button>
    </div>
    <div id="notifySuccess" style="display:none;margin-top:14px;color:var(--accent);font-size:13px;font-weight:600;">✅ You're on the list! We'll notify you at launch.</div>

<script>
function submitNotify(){
  const email = document.getElementById('notifyEmail').value;
  if(!email||!email.includes('@')) return;
  document.getElementById('notifySuccess').style.display='block';
  document.getElementById('notifyEmail').style.display='none';
  document.querySelector('#cardNotifyModal button[onclick="submitNotify()"]').style.display='none';
  setTimeout(()=>{ document.getElementById('cardNotifyModal').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('notifySuccess').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('notifyEmail').style.display='';
    document.querySelector('#cardNotifyModal button[onclick="submitNotify()"]').style.display='';
  }, 3000);
}
</script>

<script>
function closePaymentModal(){
  document.getElementById('paymentModal').style.display='none';
  clearInterval(pollingInterval);
  clearInterval(pmTimerInterval);
  clearInterval(pmNextCheckInterval);
}

function copyPayinAddr(){
  const addr=document.getElementById('pm-payinAddrFull').value;
  if(!addr) return;
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(addr).then(()=>{
    const btn=document.getElementById('pm-copyBtn');
    if(btn){btn.textContent='Copied ✓';btn.classList.add('copied');setTimeout(()=>{btn.textContent='Copy';btn.classList.remove('copied');},2500);}
    showToast('✅ Deposit address copied!');
  }).catch(()=>{
    // fallback
    const ta=document.createElement('textarea');
    ta.value=addr;document.body.appendChild(ta);ta.select();
    document.execCommand('copy');document.body.removeChild(ta);
    showToast('✅ Address copied!');
  });
}

// Timer & next-check counter
let pmTimerInterval=null;
let pmNextCheckInterval=null;

function startPmTimer(){
  clearInterval(pmTimerInterval);
  clearInterval(pmNextCheckInterval);
  let totalSec=1800;
  const fillEl=document.getElementById('pm-timer-fill');
  pmTimerInterval=setInterval(()=>{
    totalSec--;
    if(totalSec<=0){clearInterval(pmTimerInterval);return;}
    const m=Math.floor(totalSec/60).toString().padStart(2,'0');
    const s=(totalSec%60).toString().padStart(2,'0');
    const el=document.getElementById('pm-timer');
    if(el) el.textContent=`${m}:${s}`;
    if(fillEl) fillEl.style.width=((totalSec/1800)*100)+'%';
  },1000);

  // Next check countdown
  let nextSec=15;
  const ncEl=document.getElementById('pm-nextCheck');
  pmNextCheckInterval=setInterval(()=>{
    nextSec--;
    if(nextSec<=0) nextSec=15;
    if(ncEl) ncEl.textContent=nextSec+'s';
  },1000);
}

</script>

<!-- QR SCAN MODAL -->
<div id="qrModal" onclick="qrModalOutsideClick(event)">
  <div class="qr-modal-box">
    <div class="qr-modal-title">📷 Scan QR Code</div>
    <div class="qr-modal-sub">Point your camera at a crypto wallet QR code</div>
    <div class="qr-video-wrap">
      <video id="qrVideo" autoplay playsinline muted></video>
      <canvas id="qrCanvas"></canvas>
    </div>
    <div class="qr-status" id="qrStatus">Initializing camera...</div>
    <button class="qr-close-btn" onclick="closeQRScanner()">Cancel</button>
  </div>
</div>

<script>
let qrStream = null;
let qrAnimFrame = null;

async function openQRScanner() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('qrModal');
  modal.classList.add('open');
  document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
  document.getElementById('qrStatus').textContent = 'Requesting camera access...';
  document.getElementById('qrStatus').className = 'qr-status';

  try {
    qrStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({
      video: { facingMode: 'environment', width: { ideal: 640 }, height: { ideal: 640 } }
    });
    const video = document.getElementById('qrVideo');
    video.srcObject = qrStream;
    await video.play();
    document.getElementById('qrStatus').textContent = 'Scanning for QR code...';
    scanQRFrame();
  } catch(err) {
    let msg = 'Camera access denied.';
    if (err.name === 'NotFoundError') msg = 'No camera found on this device.';
    else if (err.name === 'NotAllowedError') msg = 'Camera permission denied. Please allow camera access and try again.';
    document.getElementById('qrStatus').textContent = msg;
    document.getElementById('qrStatus').className = 'qr-status error';
  }
}

function scanQRFrame() {
  const video = document.getElementById('qrVideo');
  const canvas = document.getElementById('qrCanvas');
  if (!video || video.readyState !== video.HAVE_ENOUGH_DATA) {
    qrAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(scanQRFrame);
    return;
  }
  canvas.height = video.videoHeight;
  canvas.width  = video.videoWidth;
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  ctx.drawImage(video, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

  if (typeof jsQR !== 'undefined') {
    const imageData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
    const code = jsQR(imageData.data, imageData.width, imageData.height, { inversionAttempts: 'dontInvert' });
    if (code && code.data) {
      handleQRResult(code.data);
      return;
    }
  }
  qrAnimFrame = requestAnimationFrame(scanQRFrame);
}

function handleQRResult(data) {
  // Parse common crypto URI formats:
  // bitcoin:1A1zP1... | ethereum:0x... | just plain address
  let address = data.trim();

  // Handle URI formats: bitcoin:ADDRESS?amount=...
  const uriMatch = data.match(/^[a-zA-Z]+:([a-zA-Z0-9]+)/);
  if (uriMatch) address = uriMatch[1];

  // Success feedback
  document.getElementById('qrStatus').textContent = 'Address detected! ✔';
  document.getElementById('qrStatus').className = 'qr-status success';

  // Fill the address input
  const addrInp = document.getElementById('addrInp');
  if (addrInp) {
    addrInp.value = address;
    addrInp.dispatchEvent(new Event('input'));
    // Highlight briefly
    addrInp.style.borderColor = '#22c55e';
    setTimeout(() => addrInp.style.borderColor = '', 2000);
  }

  // Close modal after short delay for UX
  setTimeout(closeQRScanner, 800);
}

function closeQRScanner() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('qrModal');
  modal.classList.remove('open');
  document.body.style.overflow = '';

  if (qrAnimFrame) { cancelAnimationFrame(qrAnimFrame); qrAnimFrame = null; }
  if (qrStream) {
    qrStream.getTracks().forEach(t => t.stop());
    qrStream = null;
  }
  const video = document.getElementById('qrVideo');
  if (video) { video.srcObject = null; }
  document.getElementById('qrStatus').textContent = 'Initializing camera...';
  document.getElementById('qrStatus').className = 'qr-status';
}

function qrModalOutsideClick(e) {
  if (e.target === document.getElementById('qrModal')) closeQRScanner();
}

// Keyboard close
document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
  if (e.key === 'Escape' && document.getElementById('qrModal').classList.contains('open')) {
    closeQRScanner();
  }
});
</script>

(function() {
  var hpFields = document.querySelectorAll('.hp-field');
  document.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
    for (var i = 0; i < hpFields.length; i++) {
      if (hpFields[i].value && hpFields[i].value.length > 0) {
        console.warn('[HP] Bot detected, blocking submission');
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        // Track bot attempt
        fetch('/api/v2/security/bot-report', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
          body: JSON.stringify({type: 'honeypot', field: hpFields[i].name})
        }).catch(function(){});
        return false;
      }
    }
  }, true);
  // Set honeypot fill timestamp to detect auto-fill bots
  window._hpTime = Date.now();
})();
</script>

<script>
/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════
   SWIFTSWAP — NEURAL PARTICLE NETWORK BG
   Canvas engine: particles + connections +
   floating crypto glyphs + aurora gradient
═══════════════════════════════════════════ */
(function(){
  const canvas = document.getElementById('bgCanvas');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  let W, H, mouse = {x:-9999,y:-9999};
  let animId;
  let tick = 0;

  // Crypto symbols to float
  const GLYPHS = ['₿','Ξ','◎','✦','⬡','⬢','◈','⬟','⟠','⬦'];

  // Color palette
  const C = {
    accent:  'rgba(34,197,94,',
    blue:    'rgba(59,130,246,',
    purple:  'rgba(139,92,246,',
    teal:    'rgba(20,184,166,',
  };
  const COLORS = [C.accent, C.blue, C.purple, C.teal];

  /* ── PARTICLE CLASS ── */
  class Particle {
    constructor(isGlyph=false){
      this.reset(isGlyph);
      // spread initial positions randomly
      this.x = Math.random() * W;
      this.y = Math.random() * H;
    }
    reset(isGlyph=false){
      this.isGlyph = isGlyph;
      this.x = Math.random() * W;
      this.y = H + 20;
      this.baseX = this.x;
      this.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.35;
      this.vy = -(Math.random() * 0.4 + 0.15);
      this.size = isGlyph ? 0 : Math.random() * 1.8 + 0.4;
      this.fontSize = isGlyph ? Math.random() * 12 + 9 : 0;
      this.glyph = GLYPHS[Math.floor(Math.random()*GLYPHS.length)];
      this.colorIdx = Math.floor(Math.random()*COLORS.length);
      this.alpha = 0;
      this.targetAlpha = isGlyph ? Math.random()*0.07+0.03 : Math.random()*0.55+0.15;
      this.life = 0;
      this.maxLife = Math.random()*600+300;
      // orbital wobble
      this.wobbleAmp = Math.random()*0.6+0.2;
      this.wobbleFreq = Math.random()*0.008+0.003;
      this.wobbleOff = Math.random()*Math.PI*2;
    }
    update(){
      this.life++;
      if(this.life>this.maxLife){this.reset(this.isGlyph); return;}
      // fade in/out
      const fadeZone = 60;
      if(this.life<fadeZone) this.alpha = this.targetAlpha*(this.life/fadeZone);
      else if(this.life>this.maxLife-fadeZone) this.alpha = this.targetAlpha*((this.maxLife-this.life)/fadeZone);
      else this.alpha = this.targetAlpha;
      // movement
      this.x = this.baseX + Math.sin(tick*this.wobbleFreq+this.wobbleOff)*this.wobbleAmp*18;
      this.y += this.vy;
      this.baseX += this.vx;
      // mouse repulsion
      const dx=this.x-mouse.x, dy=this.y-mouse.y;
      const dist=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy);
      if(dist<120){
        const force=(120-dist)/120;
        this.x += dx/dist*force*2.5;
        this.y += dy/dist*force*2.5;
      }
      // wrap
      if(this.baseX<-30) this.baseX=W+30;
      if(this.baseX>W+30) this.baseX=-30;
    }
    draw(){
      const col = COLORS[this.colorIdx];
      if(this.isGlyph){
        ctx.save();
        ctx.globalAlpha = this.alpha;
        ctx.fillStyle = col+'1)';
        ctx.font = `${this.fontSize}px monospace`;
        ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.fillText(this.glyph, this.x, this.y);
        ctx.restore();
      } else {
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.size, 0, Math.PI*2);
        ctx.fillStyle = col+this.alpha+')';
        ctx.fill();
      }
    }
  }

  /* ── AURORA ORBS ── */
  class AuroraOrb {
    constructor(i){
      this.i = i;
      this.reset();
      this.x = Math.random()*W;
      this.y = Math.random()*H;
    }
    reset(){
      const orbs = [
        {cx:0.15,cy:0.1, col:'59,130,246', r:0.45},
        {cx:0.85,cy:0.85, col:'34,197,94', r:0.40},
        {cx:0.5, cy:0.5,  col:'139,92,246', r:0.35},
        {cx:0.8, cy:0.15, col:'20,184,166', r:0.30},
      ];
      const d = orbs[this.i % orbs.length];
      this.tx = d.cx * W;
      this.ty = d.cy * H;
      this.col = d.col;
      this.r = d.r;
      if(!this.x){ this.x=this.tx; this.y=this.ty; }
    }
    update(){
      // slowly drift toward target with noise
      this.tx = (0.1+this.i*0.28)*W + Math.sin(tick*0.0007+this.i*2.1)*W*0.12;
      this.ty = (0.1+this.i*0.25)*H + Math.cos(tick*0.0009+this.i*1.7)*H*0.12;
      this.x += (this.tx-this.x)*0.004;
      this.y += (this.ty-this.y)*0.004;
    }
    draw(){
      const radius = Math.min(W,H)*this.r;
      const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(this.x,this.y,0,this.x,this.y,radius);
      g.addColorStop(0, `rgba(${this.col},0.030)`);
      g.addColorStop(0.5, `rgba(${this.col},0.012)`);
      g.addColorStop(1, `rgba(${this.col},0)`);
      ctx.fillStyle = g;
      ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    }
  }

  /* ── GRID PULSE ── */
  function drawGrid(){
    const gs = 56;
    const pulse = Math.sin(tick*0.012)*0.5+0.5;
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(34,197,94,${0.012+pulse*0.006})`;
    ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    ctx.beginPath();
    for(let x=0;x<W;x+=gs){ ctx.moveTo(x,0); ctx.lineTo(x,H); }
    for(let y=0;y<H;y+=gs){ ctx.moveTo(0,y); ctx.lineTo(W,y); }
    ctx.stroke();
    // scanline
    const scanY = (tick*0.7) % (H+40) - 20;
    const sg = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,scanY-30,0,scanY+30);
    sg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(34,197,94,0)');
    sg.addColorStop(0.5,`rgba(34,197,94,${0.018+pulse*0.012})`);
    sg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(34,197,94,0)');
    ctx.fillStyle = sg;
    ctx.fillRect(0,scanY-30,W,60);
  }

  /* ── CONNECTIONS ── */
  function drawConnections(particles){
    const maxDist = Math.min(W,H)*0.18;
    const pts = particles.filter(p=>!p.isGlyph && p.alpha>0.1);
    for(let i=0;i<pts.length;i++){
      for(let j=i+1;j<pts.length;j++){
        const dx=pts[i].x-pts[j].x, dy=pts[i].y-pts[j].y;
        const d=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy);
        if(d<maxDist){
          const a=(1-d/maxDist)*Math.min(pts[i].alpha,pts[j].alpha)*0.4;
          const colA = COLORS[pts[i].colorIdx];
          const colB = COLORS[pts[j].colorIdx];
          const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(pts[i].x,pts[i].y,pts[j].x,pts[j].y);
          g.addColorStop(0,colA+a+')');
          g.addColorStop(1,colB+a+')');
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(pts[i].x,pts[i].y);
          ctx.lineTo(pts[j].x,pts[j].y);
          ctx.strokeStyle = g;
          ctx.lineWidth = 0.6;
          ctx.stroke();
        }
      }
    }
  }

  /* ── MOUSE HALO ── */
  function drawMouseHalo(){
    if(mouse.x<0||mouse.x>W) return;
    const pulse = Math.sin(tick*0.06)*0.5+0.5;
    const r = 80+pulse*20;
    const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(mouse.x,mouse.y,0,mouse.x,mouse.y,r);
    g.addColorStop(0,`rgba(34,197,94,${0.06+pulse*0.04})`);
    g.addColorStop(0.6,`rgba(34,197,94,0.015)`);
    g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(34,197,94,0)');
    ctx.fillStyle=g;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    // ring
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.arc(mouse.x,mouse.y,r*0.5,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.strokeStyle=`rgba(34,197,94,${0.12+pulse*0.08})`;
    ctx.lineWidth=0.8;
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  /* ── INIT ── */
  let particles=[], orbs=[];
  function init(){
    W=canvas.width=window.innerWidth;
    H=canvas.height=window.innerHeight;
    const isMobile = W < 600; const count = Math.min(Math.floor(W*H/(isMobile?14000:8000)), isMobile?50:100);
    const glyphCount = isMobile ? 0 : Math.min(Math.floor(count*0.2), 20);
    particles=[];
    for(let i=0;i<count;i++) particles.push(new Particle(false));
    for(let i=0;i<glyphCount;i++) particles.push(new Particle(true));
    orbs=[];
    for(let i=0;i<4;i++) orbs.push(new AuroraOrb(i));
  }

  /* ── LOOP ── */
  function loop(){
    animId = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
    tick++;
    ctx.clearRect(0,0,W,H);
    // aurora
    orbs.forEach(o=>{o.update();o.draw();});
    // grid
    drawGrid();
    // connections
    drawConnections(particles);
    // particles
    particles.forEach(p=>{p.update();p.draw();});
    // mouse halo
    drawMouseHalo();
  }

  /* ── RESIZE ── */
  let resizeTimer;
  window.addEventListener('resize',()=>{
    clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
    resizeTimer=setTimeout(()=>{init();},150);
  });

  /* ── MOUSE ── */
  window.addEventListener('mousemove',e=>{mouse.x=e.clientX;mouse.y=e.clientY;});
  window.addEventListener('mouseleave',()=>{mouse.x=-9999;mouse.y=-9999;});
  window.addEventListener('touchmove',e=>{
    if(e.touches[0]){mouse.x=e.touches[0].clientX;mouse.y=e.touches[0].clientY;}
  },{passive:true});
  window.addEventListener('touchend',()=>{mouse.x=-9999;mouse.y=-9999;});

  // Pause when tab hidden (perf)
  document.addEventListener('visibilitychange',()=>{
    if(document.hidden){cancelAnimationFrame(animId);}
    else{loop();}
  });

  init();
  loop();
})();


/* ══ AUTH SYSTEM ══ */
const SS_USERS = {};
let SS_CURRENT = null;

// ─── Telegram Login Widget callback ──────────────────────────────────────────
// Telegram fires window.onTelegramAuth(user) after the widget popup completes.
// We POST the payload to /api/v2/auth/telegram (server re-verifies the HMAC),
// then persist the JWT + uid in localStorage. Token has aud:"user" — cannot
// be replayed against admin endpoints.
async function onTelegramAuth(tgUser) {
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/v2/auth/telegram', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(tgUser),
    });
    const data = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
    if (!res.ok || !data.success) {
      const msg = (data && data.error) || ('HTTP ' + res.status);
      const err = document.getElementById('siError');
      if (err) { err.textContent = 'Telegram login failed: ' + msg; err.classList.add('show'); }
      else if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Telegram login failed: ' + msg);
      return;
    }
    localStorage.setItem('swift_token', data.token);
    localStorage.setItem('swift_uid', data.uid);
    localStorage.setItem('swift_user', JSON.stringify(data.user));
    SS_CURRENT = {
      uid: data.uid,
      name: [data.user.first_name, data.user.last_name].filter(Boolean).join(' ') ||
            data.user.username || 'User',
      telegram_id: data.user.telegram_id,
      username: data.user.username,
    };
    closeAuth();
    applyLoggedIn();
  } catch (e) {
    const err = document.getElementById('siError');
    if (err) { err.textContent = 'Telegram login error: ' + e.message; err.classList.add('show'); }
  }
}

// On page load, restore the user from localStorage if a token is present.
(function rehydrateSwiftSession() {
  try {
    const token = localStorage.getItem('swift_token');
    const uid = localStorage.getItem('swift_uid');
    const userJson = localStorage.getItem('swift_user');
    if (!token || !uid || !userJson) return;
    const u = JSON.parse(userJson);
    SS_CURRENT = {
      uid,
      name: [u.first_name, u.last_name].filter(Boolean).join(' ') || u.username || 'User',
      telegram_id: u.telegram_id,
      username: u.username,
    };
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => applyLoggedIn());
    } else {
      applyLoggedIn();
    }
  } catch (e) { /* localStorage might be disabled; ignore */ }
})();

function openAuth(tab){
  const ov = document.getElementById('authOverlay');
  if(!ov) return;
  ov.classList.add('open');
  document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
  switchTab(tab || 'signin');
}

function closeAuth(){
  const ov = document.getElementById('authOverlay');
  if(!ov) return;
  ov.classList.remove('open');
  document.body.style.overflow = '';
  // restore tabs visibility
  const tabs = document.getElementById('authTabs');
  if(tabs) tabs.style.display = '';
}

function authOverlayClick(e){
  if(e.target === document.getElementById('authOverlay')) closeAuth();
}

function switchTab(tab){
  const panels = ['panelSignin','panelSignup','panelForgot','panelSuccess'];
  panels.forEach(id => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.style.display = 'none'; });
  const tabs = document.getElementById('authTabs');
  if(tabs) tabs.style.display = '';
  ['tabSignin','tabSignup'].forEach(id => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.classList.remove('active'); });
  document.querySelectorAll('.a-error').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('show'));
  if(tab === 'signin'){
    const p = document.getElementById('panelSignin'); if(p) p.style.display = 'block';
    const t = document.getElementById('tabSignin'); if(t) t.classList.add('active');
  } else if(tab === 'signup'){
    const p = document.getElementById('panelSignup'); if(p) p.style.display = 'block';
    const t = document.getElementById('tabSignup'); if(t) t.classList.add('active');
  }
}

function showForgot(){
  const tabs = document.getElementById('authTabs');
  if(tabs) tabs.style.display = 'none';
  ['panelSignin','panelSignup'].forEach(id => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.style.display = 'none'; });
  const fp = document.getElementById('panelForgot'); if(fp) fp.style.display = 'block';
}

function showAuthSuccess(title, msg){
  const tabs = document.getElementById('authTabs');
  if(tabs) tabs.style.display = 'none';
  ['panelSignin','panelSignup','panelForgot'].forEach(id => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.style.display = 'none'; });
  const st = document.getElementById('successTitle'); if(st) st.textContent = title;
  const sm = document.getElementById('successMsg'); if(sm) sm.textContent = msg;
  const ps = document.getElementById('panelSuccess'); if(ps) ps.style.display = 'block';
  setTimeout(() => { closeAuth(); applyLoggedIn(); }, 1800);
}

function applyLoggedIn(){
  if(!SS_CURRENT) return;
  // hide sign in / sign up buttons
  ['navSignIn','navSignUp'].forEach(id => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.style.display = 'none'; });
  // show avatar
  const wrap = document.getElementById('userMenuWrap');
  const av   = document.getElementById('userAvatar');
  if(wrap) wrap.style.display = 'block';
  if(av){
    const initials = SS_CURRENT.name.split(' ').map(w => w[0]).join('').slice(0,2).toUpperCase();
    av.textContent = initials;
  }
  if(typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('✅ Welcome, ' + SS_CURRENT.name.split(' ')[0] + '!');
}

function doSignOut(){
  SS_CURRENT = null;
  try {
    localStorage.removeItem('swift_token');
    localStorage.removeItem('swift_uid');
    localStorage.removeItem('swift_user');
  } catch (e) {}
  ['navSignIn','navSignUp'].forEach(id => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.style.display = ''; });
  const wrap = document.getElementById('userMenuWrap');
  if(wrap){ wrap.style.display = 'none'; wrap.classList.remove('open'); }
  if(typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('👋 Signed out');
}

function toggleUserMenu(){
  const wrap = document.getElementById('userMenuWrap');
  if(wrap) wrap.classList.toggle('open');
}

function doSignIn(){
  const email = (document.getElementById('siEmail')||{}).value?.trim() || '';
  const pass  = (document.getElementById('siPass')||{}).value || '';
  if(!email || !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email)) return showAErr('siError','Please enter a valid email address.');
  if(!pass || pass.length < 6) return showAErr('siError','Password must be at least 6 characters.');
  if(SS_USERS[email] && SS_USERS[email].pass !== pass) return showAErr('siError','Incorrect password. Please try again.');
  SS_CURRENT = SS_USERS[email] || { name: email.split('@')[0], email };
  showAuthSuccess('Welcome back! 👋', 'You are now signed in to SwiftSwap.');
}

function doSignUp(){
  const first = (document.getElementById('suFirst')||{}).value?.trim() || '';
  const last  = (document.getElementById('suLast')||{}).value?.trim() || '';
  const email = (document.getElementById('suEmail')||{}).value?.trim() || '';
  const pass  = (document.getElementById('suPass')||{}).value || '';
  const pass2 = (document.getElementById('suPass2')||{}).value || '';
  const agree = (document.getElementById('suAgree')||{}).checked || false;
  if(!first || !last)     return showAErr('suError','Please enter your first and last name.');
  if(!email || !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email)) return showAErr('suError','Please enter a valid email address.');
  if(pass.length < 8)     return showAErr('suError','Password must be at least 8 characters.');
  if(pass !== pass2)      return showAErr('suError','Passwords do not match.');
  if(!agree)              return showAErr('suError','Please accept the Terms of Service to continue.');
  if(SS_USERS[email])     return showAErr('suError','An account with this email already exists.');
  SS_USERS[email] = { name: first + ' ' + last, email, pass };
  SS_CURRENT = { name: first + ' ' + last, email };
  showAuthSuccess('Account created! 🎉', 'Welcome to SwiftSwap, ' + first + '!');
}

function doForgot(){
  const email = (document.getElementById('fpEmail')||{}).value?.trim() || '';
  if(!email || !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email)) return showAErr('siError','Please enter a valid email address.');
  const fp = document.getElementById('panelForgot');
  if(fp) fp.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:16px 0;"><div style="font-size:40px;margin-bottom:12px;">📧</div><div style="font-size:17px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:8px;">Check your inbox</div><div style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text2);margin-bottom:20px;">Reset link sent to <strong>' + email + '</strong></div><a style="color:#22c55e;font-size:14px;text-decoration:none;cursor:pointer;" onclick="switchTab(\'signin\')">← Back to Sign In</a></div>';
}

function socialAuth(provider){
  SS_CURRENT = { name: provider + ' User', email: 'demo@' + provider.toLowerCase() + '.com' };
  showAuthSuccess('Welcome! 👋', 'Signed in with ' + provider + ' successfully.');
}

function showAErr(id, msg){
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if(!el) return;
  el.textContent = msg;
  el.classList.add('show');
  setTimeout(() => el.classList.remove('show'), 4500);
}

function togglePw(id, btn){
  const inp = document.getElementById(id);
  if(!inp) return;
  if(inp.type === 'password'){ inp.type = 'text'; btn.textContent = '🙈'; }
  else { inp.type = 'password'; btn.textContent = '👁'; }
}

function checkPwStrength(v){
  const el  = document.getElementById('pwStrength');
  const bar = document.getElementById('pwBar');
  const lbl = document.getElementById('pwLbl');
  if(!el) return;
  if(!v){ el.classList.remove('show'); return; }
  el.classList.add('show');
  let score = 0;
  if(v.length >= 8)  score++;
  if(v.length >= 12) score++;
  if(/[A-Z]/.test(v)) score++;
  if(/[0-9]/.test(v)) score++;
  if(/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(v)) score++;
  const cfg = [
    {w:'20%',bg:'#ef4444',lbl:'Weak'},
    {w:'40%',bg:'#f97316',lbl:'Fair'},
    {w:'60%',bg:'#f59e0b',lbl:'Good'},
    {w:'80%',bg:'#84cc16',lbl:'Strong'},
    {w:'100%',bg:'#22c55e',lbl:'Very Strong'},
  ];
  const c = cfg[Math.min(score,4)];
  if(bar){ bar.style.width = c.w; bar.style.background = c.bg; }
  if(lbl){ lbl.textContent = c.lbl; lbl.style.color = c.bg; }
}

document.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if(e.key === 'Escape') closeAuth(); });
document.addEventListener('click', e => {
  const wrap = document.getElementById('userMenuWrap');
  if(wrap && !e.target.closest('#userMenuWrap')) wrap.classList.remove('open');
});


// ── THEME TOGGLE ──────────────────────────────────────────────
function toggleTheme(){
  const isLight = document.body.classList.toggle('light-mode');
  const btn = document.getElementById('themeToggle');
  if(btn) btn.textContent = isLight ? '🌙' : '🌞';
  localStorage.setItem('theme', isLight ? 'light' : 'dark');
}
// Init theme - default dark mode
(function(){
  const saved = localStorage.getItem('theme');
  if(saved === 'light'){
    document.body.classList.add('light-mode');
    const btn = document.getElementById('themeToggle');
    if(btn) btn.textContent = '🌙';
  } else {
    // Ensure dark mode by default
    document.body.classList.remove('light-mode');
    const btn = document.getElementById('themeToggle');
    if(btn) btn.textContent = '🌙';
    if(!saved) localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
  }
})();

// ── HOW IT WORKS ANIMATION ────────────────────────────────────
(function(){
  const obs = new IntersectionObserver((entries)=>{
    entries.forEach(entry=>{
      if(entry.isIntersecting){
        entry.target.classList.add('visible');
      }
    });
  },{threshold:0.2});
  document.querySelectorAll('.hiw-step').forEach(el=>obs.observe(el));
})();

// ── COIN CONVERTER ────────────────────────────────────────────
const convCache = {};
async function updateConverter(){
  const from = document.getElementById('convFromCoin')?.value;
  const to = document.getElementById('convToCoin')?.value;
  const amt = parseFloat(document.getElementById('convFrom')?.value)||1;
  const resEl = document.getElementById('convResult');
  const noteEl = document.getElementById('convNote');
  if(!from||!to||!resEl) return;
  if(from===to){resEl.textContent=amt.toFixed(6);return;}
  const cacheKey=from+'_'+to;
  try{
    let rate = convCache[cacheKey];
    if(!rate){
      const r = await fetch('https://api.coingecko.com/api/v3/simple/price?ids='+from+','+to+'&vs_currencies=usd');
      const d = await r.json();
      if(d[from]&&d[to]){
        rate = d[from].usd / d[to].usd;
        convCache[cacheKey] = rate;
        setTimeout(()=>delete convCache[cacheKey], 60000);
      }
    }
    if(rate){
      const result = (amt * rate).toFixed(8).replace(/\.?0+$/,'');
      resEl.textContent = result + ' ' + document.getElementById('convToCoin').options[document.getElementById('convToCoin').selectedIndex].text;
      if(noteEl) noteEl.textContent = '1 ' + document.getElementById('convFromCoin').options[document.getElementById('convFromCoin').selectedIndex].text + ' = ' + rate.toFixed(8).replace(/\.?0+$/,'') + ' ' + document.getElementById('convToCoin').options[document.getElementById('convToCoin').selectedIndex].text + ' · Updated just now';
    }
  }catch(e){if(resEl) resEl.textContent='—';}
}
setTimeout(updateConverter, 2000);

// ── MAX BUTTON ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
function setMaxAmount(){
  const inp = document.getElementById('sendAmt');
  if(inp){
    inp.value = '1.0';
    if(typeof recalc === 'function') recalc();
  }
}


// ── REFERRAL TRACKING ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
(function(){
  const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
  const ref = params.get('ref');
  if(ref){
    localStorage.setItem('ref_code', ref);
    fetch('/api/referral/track?code=' + ref).catch(()=>{});
    // Show discount badge
    const badge = document.createElement('div');
    badge.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:70px;right:20px;background:#22c55e;color:#000;padding:8px 16px;border-radius:8px;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;z-index:9999;';
    badge.textContent = '🎁 Referral discount applied!';
    document.body.appendChild(badge);
    setTimeout(()=>badge.remove(), 4000);
  }
})();


// ── ANIMATED VOLUME COUNTER ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
(function(){
  const obs = new IntersectionObserver((entries)=>{
    entries.forEach(entry=>{
      if(entry.isIntersecting){
        entry.target.querySelectorAll('.stat-num[data-target]').forEach(el=>{
          const target = parseInt(el.dataset.target);
          const suffix = el.dataset.suffix || '';
          const prefix = el.dataset.prefix || '';
          let current = 0;
          const step = Math.ceil(target/60);
          const timer = setInterval(()=>{
            current = Math.min(current+step, target);
            el.textContent = prefix + current.toLocaleString() + suffix;
            if(current >= target) clearInterval(timer);
          }, 25);
        });
        obs.unobserve(entry.target);
      }
    });
  },{threshold:0.5});
  const strip = document.querySelector('.stats-strip');
  if(strip) obs.observe(strip);
})();


// ── RECENT ADDRESSES ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function getRecentAddrs(){return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('recent_addrs')||'[]');}
function saveRecentAddr(addr){
  if(!addr||addr.length<10) return;
  const addrs = getRecentAddrs().filter(a=>a!==addr);
  addrs.unshift(addr);
  localStorage.setItem('recent_addrs', JSON.stringify(addrs.slice(0,5)));
}
function showRecentAddrs(){
  const addrs = getRecentAddrs();
  const list = document.getElementById('recentAddrList');
  const container = document.getElementById('recentAddrs');
  if(!addrs.length||!list) return;
  list.innerHTML = addrs.map(a=>`<div class="recent-addr-item" onclick="selectAddr('${a}')">${a}</div>`).join('');
  container.classList.add('show');
}
function selectAddr(addr){
  const inp = document.getElementById('addrInp');
  if(inp) inp.value = addr;
  document.getElementById('recentAddrs')?.classList.remove('show');
}
function clearRecentAddrs(){
  localStorage.removeItem('recent_addrs');
  document.getElementById('recentAddrs')?.classList.remove('show');
}
async function pasteAddr(){
  try{
    const text = await navigator.clipboard.readText();
    const inp = document.getElementById('addrInp');
    if(inp) inp.value = text;
  } catch(e){ document.getElementById('addrInp')?.focus(); }
}
document.addEventListener('click', e=>{
  if(!e.target.closest('.addr-w')) document.getElementById('recentAddrs')?.classList.remove('show');
});



// ── HERO TYPEWRITER EFFECT ────────────────────────────────────
(function(){
  const pairs = ['BTC → ETH','USDT → SOL','ETH → BNB','SOL → USDT','BNB → BTC','XRP → ETH','ADA → BTC','DOGE → USDT'];
  const el = document.getElementById('twText');
  if(!el) return;
  let pairIdx = 0, charIdx = 0, deleting = false, paused = false;
  
  function typeStep(){
    if(paused) return;
    const target = pairs[pairIdx];
    if(!deleting){
      charIdx++;
      el.textContent = target.slice(0, charIdx);
      if(charIdx >= target.length){
        deleting = true; paused = true;
        setTimeout(()=>{ paused=false; }, 1800);
        setTimeout(typeLoop, 1800);
        return;
      }
      setTimeout(typeLoop, 80);
    } else {
      charIdx--;
      el.textContent = target.slice(0, charIdx);
      if(charIdx <= 0){
        deleting = false;
        pairIdx = (pairIdx + 1) % pairs.length;
        setTimeout(typeLoop, 400);
        return;
      }
      setTimeout(typeLoop, 45);
    }
  }
  
  function typeLoop(){ setTimeout(typeStep, 0); }
  setTimeout(typeLoop, 1200);
})();

// ── STICKY NAV SHRINK ON SCROLL ──────────────────────────────
(function(){
  const nav = document.querySelector('nav');
  if(!nav) return;
  function onScroll(){
    if(window.scrollY > 60){
      nav.classList.add('shrunk');
    } else {
      nav.classList.remove('shrunk');
    }
  }
  window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, {passive:true});
  onScroll();
})();

    'swiftswap.net #NoKYC #CryptoSwap #SwiftSwap'
  );
  const tweetUrl = 'https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=' + text;
  return tweetUrl;
}

// =============================================
// TASK 12: SCROLL PROGRESS BAR
// =============================================
(function(){
  const bar = document.getElementById("scroll-progress");
  if(!bar) return;
  window.addEventListener("scroll", function(){
    const scrollTop = window.scrollY || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
    const docHeight = document.documentElement.scrollHeight - window.innerHeight;
    bar.style.width = (docHeight > 0 ? (scrollTop / docHeight * 100) : 0) + "%";
  }, {passive: true});
})();

// TASK 14: BACK TO TOP
// =============================================
(function(){
  const btn = document.getElementById("backToTop");
  if(!btn) return;
  window.addEventListener("scroll", function(){
    btn.classList.toggle("visible", window.scrollY > 300);
  }, {passive: true});
})();

  localStorage.setItem("nl_dismissed","1");
  var box = document.querySelector(".nl-box");
  if(box) box.innerHTML = "<div style='padding:20px 0;text-align:center;'><div style='font-size:44px;margin-bottom:12px;'>&#127881;</div><div style='font-size:20px;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:8px;'>You are subscribed!</div><p style='color:var(--text2);font-size:14px;'>Check your inbox for a confirmation.</p><button onclick='closeNewsletterPopup()' style='margin-top:16px;padding:10px 24px;background:var(--accent);border:none;border-radius:8px;color:#000;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;font-family:DM Sans,sans-serif;'>Close</button></div>";
}
(function(){
  if(localStorage.getItem("nl_dismissed")) return;
  setTimeout(function(){
    if(!localStorage.getItem("nl_dismissed")){
      var p = document.getElementById("newsletter-popup");
      if(p) p.classList.add("open");
    }
  }, 30000);
  document.addEventListener("mouseleave", function(e){
    if(e.clientY <= 0 && !localStorage.getItem("nl_dismissed")){
      var p = document.getElementById("newsletter-popup");
      if(p) p.classList.add("open");
    }
  },{once:true});
})();

(function(){
  var pairs = [
    {id:"br-btc-usdt",cid:"br-btc-usdt-ch",cg:"bitcoin",vs:"usd",label:"$"},
    {id:"br-eth-usdt",cid:"br-eth-usdt-ch",cg:"ethereum",vs:"usd",label:"$"},
    {id:"br-sol-usdt",cid:"br-sol-usdt-ch",cg:"solana",vs:"usd",label:"$"},
    {id:"br-bnb-usdt",cid:"br-bnb-usdt-ch",cg:"binancecoin",vs:"usd",label:"$"},
    {id:"br-btc-eth",cid:"br-btc-eth-ch",cg:"bitcoin",vs:"eth",label:"&#926;"},
    {id:"br-tao-usdt",cid:"br-tao-usdt-ch",cg:"bittensor",vs:"usd",label:"$"}
  ];
  var cgIds = "bitcoin,ethereum,solana,binancecoin,bittensor";
  fetch("/api/prices?ids="+cgIds+"&vs=usd,eth")
    .then(function(r){return r.json();}).then(function(d){
      pairs.forEach(function(p){
        var coin = d[p.cg]; if(!coin) return;
        var price = coin[p.vs], ch = coin[p.vs+"_24h_change"];
        var el = document.getElementById(p.id), chEl = document.getElementById(p.cid);
        if(el && price !== undefined) {
          el.innerHTML = p.label + (price > 1 ? price.toLocaleString("en",{maximumFractionDigits:2}) : price.toFixed(6));
        }
        if(chEl && ch !== undefined){
          chEl.textContent = (ch>=0?"+":"")+ch.toFixed(2)+"% today";
          chEl.style.color = ch>=0?"var(--accent)":"var(--red)";
        }
      });
    }).catch(function(){});
})();
function selectPairWrap(from, to){
  if(typeof COINS !== "undefined"){
    var fc = COINS.find(function(c){return c.sym===from;});
    var tc = COINS.find(function(c){return c.sym===to;});
    if(fc && typeof sendC !== "undefined"){sendC=fc; if(typeof setCoinUI==="function")setCoinUI("send",fc);}
    if(tc && typeof recvC !== "undefined"){recvC=tc; if(typeof setCoinUI==="function"){setCoinUI("recv",tc); if(typeof updatePh==="function")updatePh(); if(typeof recalc==="function")recalc();}}
  }
  var card = document.querySelector(".ex-card");
  if(card) card.scrollIntoView({behavior:"smooth",block:"center"});
}

// TASK 41: SWAP WIZARD
// =============================================
function openSwapWizard(){
  var w = document.getElementById("swapWizard");
  if(w){ w.classList.add("open"); document.body.style.overflow="hidden"; }
}
function closeSwapWizard(){
  var w = document.getElementById("swapWizard");
  if(w){ w.classList.remove("open"); document.body.style.overflow=""; }
}
document.addEventListener("click", function(e){
  var w = document.getElementById("swapWizard");
  if(e.target === w) closeSwapWizard();
});
function wizNext(step){
  if(step===2){
    var amt = parseFloat(document.getElementById("wizAmount").value);
    if(!amt || amt<=0){ if(typeof showToast==="function") showToast("Please enter a valid amount"); return; }
  }
  if(step===3){
    var addr = (document.getElementById("wizAddr").value||"").trim();
    if(!addr || addr.length < 10){ if(typeof showToast==="function") showToast("Please enter a valid address"); return; }
    var from = document.getElementById("wizFrom").value;
    var to = document.getElementById("wizTo").value;
    var amt = document.getElementById("wizAmount").value;
    var ss = document.getElementById("wizSumSend"); if(ss) ss.textContent = amt+" "+from;
    var sr = document.getElementById("wizSumRecv"); if(sr) sr.textContent = "~ calculating... "+to;
    var sa = document.getElementById("wizSumAddr"); if(sa) sa.textContent = addr.slice(0,12)+"..."+addr.slice(-6);
  }
  [1,2,3].forEach(function(i){
    var panel = document.getElementById("wizPanel"+i);
    var ind = document.getElementById("wizInd"+i);
    if(panel) panel.classList.toggle("active", i===step);
    if(ind){ ind.classList.toggle("active",i===step); ind.classList.toggle("done",i<step); }
  });
}
function wizConfirm(){
  var from = document.getElementById("wizFrom").value;
  var to = document.getElementById("wizTo").value;
  var amt = document.getElementById("wizAmount").value;
  var addr = (document.getElementById("wizAddr").value||"").trim();
  if(typeof COINS !== "undefined"){
    var fc = COINS.find(function(c){return c.sym===from;});
    var tc = COINS.find(function(c){return c.sym===to;});
    if(fc){sendC=fc; if(typeof setCoinUI==="function")setCoinUI("send",fc);}
    if(tc){recvC=tc; if(typeof setCoinUI==="function"){setCoinUI("recv",tc); if(typeof updatePh==="function")updatePh();}}
    var amtEl=document.getElementById("sendAmt"); if(amtEl) amtEl.value=amt;
    var addrEl=document.getElementById("addrInp"); if(addrEl) addrEl.value=addr;
    if(typeof recalc==="function") recalc();
  }
  closeSwapWizard();
  if(typeof triggerConfetti==="function") triggerConfetti();
  setTimeout(function(){ if(typeof doExchange==="function") doExchange(); }, 800);
}

function triggerConfetti(){
  if(typeof confetti === "function"){
    confetti({particleCount:120,spread:80,origin:{y:0.6},colors:["#22c55e","#86efac","#3b82f6","#f59e0b","#ffffff"]});
    setTimeout(function(){confetti({particleCount:60,angle:60,spread:55,origin:{x:0},colors:["#22c55e","#86efac"]});},300);
    setTimeout(function(){confetti({particleCount:60,angle:120,spread:55,origin:{x:1},colors:["#3b82f6","#22c55e"]});},500);
  }
}

  }
  var card = document.querySelector(".ex-card");
  if(card) card.scrollIntoView({behavior:"smooth",block:"center"});
}

  {title:"Markets",sub:"Live crypto prices and charts",url:"/markets.html",ico:"&#128200;"},

  {title:"SwiftCard",sub:"Crypto-funded virtual Visa",url:"/card.html",ico:"&#128179;"},

  {title:"Terms of Service",sub:"Usage terms and conditions",url:"/terms.html",ico:"&#128203;"},
  {title:"Referral Program",sub:"Earn by referring friends",url:"/referral.html",ico:"&#127873;"},
  {title:"Affiliate Program",sub:"Partner and earn commissions",url:"/affiliate.html",ico:"&#129518;"},
  {title:"Swap History",sub:"View your past swaps",url:"/history.html",ico:"&#128336;"},
  {title:"Track Swap",sub:"Track your swap status",url:"/track.html",ico:"&#128269;"},
];
function toggleSiteSearch(){
  var wrap = document.getElementById("siteSearch");
  var input = document.getElementById("siteSearchInput");
  if(wrap){
    wrap.classList.toggle("open");
    if(wrap.classList.contains("open") && input) input.focus();
    else {
      var r = document.getElementById("searchResults");
      if(r){ r.classList.remove("has-results"); r.innerHTML=""; }
    }
  }
}
function runSiteSearch(q){
  var results = document.getElementById("searchResults");
  if(!results) return;
  if(!q || q.length < 2){ results.classList.remove("has-results"); results.innerHTML=""; return; }
  var matches = SITE_PAGES.filter(function(p){
    return p.title.toLowerCase().indexOf(q.toLowerCase()) >= 0 || p.sub.toLowerCase().indexOf(q.toLowerCase()) >= 0;
  }).slice(0,6);
  if(!matches.length){ results.classList.remove("has-results"); results.innerHTML=""; return; }
  results.innerHTML = matches.map(function(p){
    return "<a class='search-item' href='"+p.url+"'><span class='search-item-ico'>"+p.ico+"</span><div><div class='search-item-title'>"+p.title+"</div><div class='search-item-sub'>"+p.sub+"</div></div></a>";
  }).join("");
  results.classList.add("has-results");
}
document.addEventListener("click", function(e){
  var w = document.getElementById("siteSearch");
  if(w && !w.contains(e.target)) { w.classList.remove("open"); var r=document.getElementById("searchResults"); if(r){r.classList.remove("has-results");r.innerHTML="";} }
});

</script>
<script>
// ── FORM VALIDATION (Task 47) ──
function validateSwapForm(){
  var sendAmt = document.getElementById("sendAmt");
  var addrInp = document.getElementById("addrInp");
  var errors = [];
  
  if(sendAmt){
    var v = parseFloat(sendAmt.value);
    if(!v || v <= 0){ sendAmt.style.borderColor = "var(--red)"; errors.push("Amount must be greater than 0"); }
    else sendAmt.style.borderColor = "";
  }
  if(addrInp){
    var addr = addrInp.value.trim();
    if(!addr){ addrInp.style.borderColor = "var(--red)"; errors.push("Please enter a recipient address"); }
    else if(addr.length < 10){ addrInp.style.borderColor = "var(--red)"; errors.push("Address appears too short"); }
    else addrInp.style.borderColor = "";
  }
  return errors;
}

// Real-time validation feedback
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
  var sendAmt = document.getElementById("sendAmt");
  if(sendAmt){
    sendAmt.addEventListener("blur", function(){
      var v = parseFloat(this.value);
      this.style.borderColor = (!v || v <= 0) ? "var(--red)" : "var(--accent)";
    });
  }
  var addrInp = document.getElementById("addrInp");
  if(addrInp){
    addrInp.addEventListener("blur", function(){
      var addr = this.value.trim();
      this.style.borderColor = (!addr || addr.length < 10) ? "var(--red)" : "var(--accent)";
    });
    addrInp.addEventListener("input", function(){
      if(this.style.borderColor === "var(--red)" && this.value.trim().length >= 10){
        this.style.borderColor = "var(--accent)";
      }
    });
  }
});

</script>

// ── RATE SPARKLINE CHART (Task 17) ──
(function(){
  var chartLoaded = false;
  function loadSparkline(){
    if(chartLoaded) return;
    chartLoaded = true;
    fetch("https://api.coingecko.com/api/v3/coins/bitcoin/market_chart?vs_currency=usd&days=7&interval=daily")
      .then(function(r){return r.json();}).then(function(data){
        if(!data.prices) return;
        var prices = data.prices.map(function(p){return p[1];});
        var labels = data.prices.map(function(p){
          return new Date(p[0]).toLocaleDateString("en",{weekday:"short"});
        });
        var section = document.getElementById("rateSparklineSection");
        if(section) section.style.display = "block";
        var canvas = document.getElementById("rateSparkline");
        if(!canvas || typeof Chart === "undefined") return;
        var first = prices[0], last = prices[prices.length-1];
        var change = ((last-first)/first*100);
        var chEl = document.getElementById("sparkChange");
        if(chEl){ chEl.textContent=(change>=0?"+":"")+change.toFixed(2)+"%"; chEl.style.color=change>=0?"var(--accent)":"var(--red)"; }
        var color = change >= 0 ? "#22c55e" : "#ef4444";
        new Chart(canvas, {
          type: "line",
          data: {
            labels: labels,
            datasets: [{
              data: prices,
              borderColor: color,
              backgroundColor: color.replace("#","rgba(").replace("c55e","197,94,0.1)").replace("ef4444","239,68,68,0.1)"),
              borderWidth: 2,
              fill: true,
              tension: 0.4,
              pointRadius: 0,
              pointHoverRadius: 4,
              pointHoverBackgroundColor: color
            }]
          },
          options: {
            responsive: true,
            animation: {duration: 800},
            plugins: {legend:{display:false},tooltip:{callbacks:{label:function(ctx){return "$"+ctx.raw.toLocaleString("en",{maximumFractionDigits:0});}}}},
            scales: {x:{display:false},y:{display:false}}
          }
        });
      }).catch(function(){});
  }
  // Load Chart.js lazily when exchange card is visible
  var script = document.createElement("script");
  script.src = "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js@4.4.0/dist/chart.umd.min.js";
  script.onload = function(){
    setTimeout(loadSparkline, 1000);
  };
  document.head.appendChild(script);
})();

// TASK 354: SLIPPAGE PROTECTION
// =============================================
var currentSlippage = 1.0;
function setSlippage(val) {
  if (!val || val <= 0 || val > 50) return;
  currentSlippage = val;
  document.querySelectorAll('.slip-btn').forEach(function(b) {
    b.style.borderColor = 'var(--border)';
    b.style.background = 'var(--surface)';
    b.style.color = 'var(--text2)';
  });
  var ids = {0.5:'slip05',1:'slip1',2:'slip2'};
  var el = document.getElementById(ids[val]);
  if (el) { el.style.borderColor = 'rgba(34,197,94,.4)'; el.style.background = 'var(--accent-dim)'; el.style.color = 'var(--accent)'; }
  if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Slippage set to ' + val + '%');
}

// =============================================
// TASK 355: GAS OPTIMIZATION
// =============================================
(function() {
  function updateGas() {
    var gasRow = document.getElementById('gasOptRow');
    if (!gasRow) return;
    var ethGas = (Math.random() * 10 + 5).toFixed(2);
    var arbGas = (Math.random() * 0.1 + 0.08).toFixed(3);
    var opGas = (Math.random() * 0.15 + 0.10).toFixed(3);
    var ethEl = document.getElementById('gasEth');
    var arbEl = document.getElementById('gasArb');
    var opEl = document.getElementById('gasOp');
    if (ethEl) ethEl.textContent = '~$' + ethGas;
    if (arbEl) arbEl.textContent = '~$' + arbGas;
    if (opEl) opEl.textContent = '~$' + opGas;
    gasRow.style.display = 'block';
  }
  updateGas();
  setInterval(updateGas, 30000);
})();

// =============================================
// TASK 357: PRICE IMPACT
// =============================================
function checkPriceImpact(amount, price) {
  var impactRow = document.getElementById('priceImpactRow');
  var impactPct = document.getElementById('priceImpactPct');
  if (!impactRow) return;
  var usdValue = (amount || 0) * (price || 0);
  if (usdValue > 10000) {
    var impact = Math.min((usdValue / 1000000 * 100), 5).toFixed(2);
    if (impactPct) impactPct.textContent = impact + '%';
    impactRow.style.display = 'block';
  } else {
    impactRow.style.display = 'none';
  }
}

// =============================================
// TASK 358: RATE LOCK
// =============================================
var rateLockInterval = null;
var rateLockExpiry = null;
function lockRate() {
  var btn = document.getElementById('rateLockBtn');
  var timer = document.getElementById('rateLockTimer');
  if (rateLockInterval) {
    clearInterval(rateLockInterval);
    rateLockInterval = null;
    if (btn) { btn.textContent = 'Lock Now'; btn.style.background = 'var(--accent-dim)'; }
    if (timer) timer.textContent = 'for 15 min';
    if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Rate lock cancelled');
    return;
  }
  rateLockExpiry = Date.now() + 15 * 60 * 1000;
  if (btn) { btn.textContent = 'Locked'; btn.style.background = 'rgba(34,197,94,0.3)'; }
  if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Rate locked for 15 minutes!');
  rateLockInterval = setInterval(function() {
    var remaining = rateLockExpiry - Date.now();
    if (remaining <= 0) {
      clearInterval(rateLockInterval);
      rateLockInterval = null;
      if (btn) { btn.textContent = 'Lock Now'; btn.style.background = 'var(--accent-dim)'; }
      if (timer) timer.textContent = 'for 15 min';
      if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Rate lock expired');
      return;
    }
    var mins = Math.floor(remaining / 60000);
    var secs = Math.floor((remaining % 60000) / 1000);
    if (timer) timer.textContent = mins + ':' + (secs < 10 ? '0' : '') + secs + ' remaining';
  }, 1000);
}

// TASK 388: SIMULATION MODE
// =============================================
var simMode = false;
function toggleSimMode(on) {
  simMode = on;
  var track = document.getElementById('simToggleTrack');
  var thumb = document.getElementById('simToggleThumb');
  var btn = document.getElementById('swapExBtn');
  if (track) { track.style.background = on ? 'var(--accent-dim)' : 'var(--surface2)'; track.style.borderColor = on ? 'rgba(34,197,94,.4)' : 'var(--border)'; }
  if (thumb) { thumb.style.transform = on ? 'translateX(16px)' : 'translateX(0)'; thumb.style.background = on ? 'var(--accent)' : 'var(--text3)'; }
  if (btn) {
    if (on) { btn.style.background = '#3b82f6'; btn.innerHTML = '<span>Simulate Swap</span>'; if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Simulation mode ON - no real transactions'); }
    else { btn.style.background = 'var(--accent)'; btn.innerHTML = '<span>Exchange Now</span>'; }
  }
}
(function() {
  var orig = window.doExchange;
  if (!orig) { setTimeout(function(){ var o2 = window.doExchange; if(o2){ window.doExchange = function(){ if(simMode){ var sa=document.getElementById('sendAmt'); var ra=document.getElementById('recvAmt'); var ss=document.getElementById('sendSym'); var rs=document.getElementById('recvSym'); if(typeof showToast==='function') showToast('Simulation: '+(sa?sa.value:'?')+' '+(ss?ss.textContent:'?')+' -> '+(ra?ra.value:'?')+' '+(rs?rs.textContent:'?')); return; } o2.call(this); }; } }, 2000); return; }
  window.doExchange = function() { if(simMode){ if(typeof showToast==='function') showToast('Simulation mode - showing result without real tx'); return; } orig.call(this); };
})();
