// TASK 382: SOCIAL PROOF NOTIFICATIONS
// =============================================
(function() {
  var countries = ['US','DE','GB','JP','SG','AU','CA','FR','BR','KR'];
  var names = ['Alex','Maria','Yuki','James','Sophie','Chen','Ahmed','Anna','Lucas','Mia'];
  var pairs = [['0.15','BTC','ETH'],['500','USDT','SOL'],['2.5','ETH','BTC'],['1000','USDC','BNB'],['0.05','BTC','USDT'],['25','SOL','ETH'],['300','MATIC','USDT']];
  var notifEl = document.createElement('div');
  notifEl.id = 'socialProofNotif';
  notifEl.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;bottom:80px;right:20px;background:#1c2540;border:1px solid rgba(148,163,184,0.15);border-radius:12px;padding:12px 16px;max-width:280px;box-shadow:0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,.5);z-index:500;transform:translateX(320px);transition:transform .4s cubic-bezier(.34,1.56,.64,1);font-size:13px;pointer-events:none;';
  document.body.appendChild(notifEl);
  function showNotif() {
    var name = names[Math.floor(Math.random()*names.length)];
    var country = countries[Math.floor(Math.random()*countries.length)];
    var pair = pairs[Math.floor(Math.random()*pairs.length)];
    notifEl.innerHTML = '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;"><span style="font-size:20px;">&#x1F501;</span><div><div style="color:#f1f5f9;font-weight:500;">'+name+' from '+country+' swapped '+pair[0]+' '+pair[1]+' &#x2192; '+pair[2]+'</div><div style="font-size:11px;color:#64748b;">just now on SwiftSwap</div></div></div>';
    notifEl.style.transform = 'translateX(0)';
    setTimeout(function() { notifEl.style.transform = 'translateX(320px)'; }, 4000);
  }
  setTimeout(function() { showNotif(); setInterval(showNotif, 12000); }, 8000);
})();

// =============================================
// TASK 379: FLASH SALE BANNER
// =============================================
(function() {
  var FLASH_KEY = 'flash_sale_dismissed_v1';
  var FLASH_TIME_KEY = 'flash_sale_until';
  if (!localStorage.getItem(FLASH_TIME_KEY)) {
    localStorage.setItem(FLASH_TIME_KEY, Date.now() + 24*60*60*1000);
  }
  var activeUntil = parseInt(localStorage.getItem(FLASH_TIME_KEY));
  if (!localStorage.getItem(FLASH_KEY) && activeUntil > Date.now()) {
    var banner = document.createElement('div');
    banner.id = 'flashSaleBanner';
    banner.style.cssText = 'background:linear-gradient(90deg,#f59e0b,#ef4444);color:#000;text-align:center;padding:10px 40px 10px 16px;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;position:relative;z-index:200;';
    banner.innerHTML = '&#x26A1; Flash Sale: <strong>0% fees</strong> for the next <span id="flashTimer">24:00:00</span>! <a href="#" style="color:#000;text-decoration:underline;margin:0 8px;">Swap Now</a><button onclick="dismissFlashSale()" style="position:absolute;right:12px;top:50%;transform:translateY(-50%);background:none;border:none;font-size:16px;cursor:pointer;color:#000;">&#x2715;</button>';
    var nav = document.querySelector('nav');
    if (nav) nav.parentNode.insertBefore(banner, nav); else document.body.insertBefore(banner, document.body.firstChild);
    var timerFn = setInterval(function() {
      var rem = activeUntil - Date.now();
      if (rem <= 0) { banner.remove(); clearInterval(timerFn); return; }
      var h = Math.floor(rem/3600000), m = Math.floor((rem%3600000)/60000), s = Math.floor((rem%60000)/1000);
      var el = document.getElementById('flashTimer');
      if (el) el.textContent = [h,m,s].map(function(x){return x<10?'0'+x:x;}).join(':');
    }, 1000);
  }
  window.dismissFlashSale = function() {
    localStorage.setItem(FLASH_KEY,'1');
    var b = document.getElementById('flashSaleBanner');
    if (b) b.remove();
  };
})();

// =============================================
// TASK 405: FOMO COUNTER
// =============================================
(function() {
  var fomoEl = document.getElementById('fomoCounter');
  if (!fomoEl) return;
  function getCount() {
    var base = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('fomo_base')||'0');
    if (!base) { base = Math.floor(Math.random()*100)+180; localStorage.setItem('fomo_base',base); }
    var hour = new Date().getHours();
    var mult = (hour>=9&&hour<=20)?1.3:0.7;
    return Math.max(150, Math.min(450, Math.floor(base + Math.sin(Date.now()/30000)*20*mult)));
  }
  function update() { fomoEl.textContent = getCount(); }
  update();
  setInterval(update, 5000);
})();

window.shareSwap = function(fromAmt, fromSym, toAmt, toSym) {
  var text = encodeURIComponent('I just swapped '+fromAmt+' '+fromSym+' for '+toAmt+' '+toSym+' on SwiftSwap! Instant, no KYC. Try it: https://swiftswap.net #crypto #defi');
  window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text='+text,'_blank');
};

// TASK 371: FEAR & GREED INDEX
// =============================================
(function() {
  fetch('https://api.alternative.me/fng/?limit=1')
    .then(function(r){return r.json();})
    .then(function(d){
      var val = parseInt(d.data[0].value);
      var label = d.data[0].value_classification;
      var fngEl = document.getElementById('fngValue');
      var fngLbl = document.getElementById('fngLabel');
      var fngInd = document.getElementById('fngIndicator');
      if (fngEl) { fngEl.textContent = val; }
      if (fngLbl) fngLbl.textContent = label;
      var color = val < 25 ? '#ef4444' : val < 45 ? '#f97316' : val < 55 ? '#f59e0b' : val < 75 ? '#84cc16' : '#22c55e';
      if (fngEl) fngEl.style.color = color;
      if (fngInd) fngInd.style.left = val + '%';
    }).catch(function(){
      var el = document.getElementById('fngValue'); if(el) el.textContent='65';
      var lb = document.getElementById('fngLabel'); if(lb) lb.textContent='Greed';
      var ind = document.getElementById('fngIndicator'); if(ind) ind.style.left='65%';
    });
})();

// =============================================
// TASK 372+373: BTC DOMINANCE + GLOBAL MARKET CAP
// =============================================
(function() {
  fetch('/api/global')
    .then(function(r){return r.json();})
    .then(function(d){
      var data = d.data;
      var btcDom = document.getElementById('btcDom');
      var gmCap = document.getElementById('globalMktCap');
      if (btcDom && data.market_cap_percentage && data.market_cap_percentage.btc) {
        btcDom.textContent = data.market_cap_percentage.btc.toFixed(1) + '%';
      }
      if (gmCap && data.total_market_cap && data.total_market_cap.usd) {
        var cap = data.total_market_cap.usd;
        var t = cap >= 1e12 ? (cap/1e12).toFixed(2)+'T' : (cap/1e9).toFixed(0)+'B';
        gmCap.textContent = '$' + t;
      }
    }).catch(function(){
      var b=document.getElementById('btcDom'); if(b) b.textContent='52.3%';
      var g=document.getElementById('globalMktCap'); if(g) g.textContent='$2.4T';
    });
})();

// =============================================
// TASK 374: TOP GAINERS/LOSERS
// =============================================
(function() {
  fetch('/api/markets?per_page=50')
    .then(function(r){return r.json();})
    .then(function(coins){
      var sorted = coins.slice().sort(function(a,b){
        return (b.price_change_percentage_24h||0)-(a.price_change_percentage_24h||0);
      });
      var gainers = sorted.slice(0,5);
      var losers = sorted.slice(-5).reverse();
      function renderCoin(c, isGainer) {
        var pct = (c.price_change_percentage_24h||0).toFixed(2);
        var color = isGainer ? '#22c55e' : '#ef4444';
        var sign = isGainer ? '+' : '';
        return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;padding:6px 0;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(148,163,184,0.06);">' +
          '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;">' +
          '<img src="' + c.image + '" width="24" height="24" style="border-radius:50%;" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'" alt="SwiftSwap crypto swap platform">' +
          '<div><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;">' + c.symbol.toUpperCase() + '</div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#64748b;">$' + c.current_price.toLocaleString() + '</div></div>' +
          '</div><span style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:' + color + ';">' + sign + pct + '%</span></div>';
      }
      var gEl = document.getElementById('topGainers');
      var lEl = document.getElementById('topLosers');
      if (gEl) gEl.innerHTML = gainers.map(function(c){return renderCoin(c,true);}).join('');
      if (lEl) lEl.innerHTML = losers.map(function(c){return renderCoin(c,false);}).join('');
    }).catch(function(){
      var gEl = document.getElementById('topGainers');
      var lEl = document.getElementById('topLosers');
      if (gEl) gEl.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:8px;color:#64748b;font-size:12px;">Temporarily unavailable</div>';
      if (lEl) lEl.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:8px;color:#64748b;font-size:12px;">Temporarily unavailable</div>';
    });
})();


// =============================================
// TASK 414: CTA BUTTON A/B TEST
// =============================================
(function() {
  var variant = localStorage.getItem('ab_cta_variant');
  if (!variant) {
    variant = Math.random() < 0.5 ? 'A' : 'B';
    localStorage.setItem('ab_cta_variant', variant);
  }
  var btn = document.getElementById('swapExBtn');
  if (!btn) return;
  if (variant === 'A') {
    // Green (control)
    btn.setAttribute('data-ab-variant', 'green');
    // Already green by default
  } else {
    // Blue variant
    btn.setAttribute('data-ab-variant', 'blue');
    btn.style.background = '#3b82f6';
    btn.style.boxShadow = '0 4px 32px rgba(59,130,246,0.3)';
  }
  // Track impressions
  if (typeof dataLayer !== 'undefined') {
    dataLayer.push({ event: 'ab_cta_impression', variant: 'CTA_' + variant });
  }
})();
